### [269] [Statistical Efficiency of Single- and Multi-step Models for Forecasting and Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23465)
*Anne Somalwar,Bruce D. Lee,George J. Pappas,Nikolai Matni*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文首次对线性动力系统中单步与多步预测器的权衡进行了定量分析，发现当模型类别正确指定时单步模型误差最低，但在部分可观测导致模型误指定时多步预测器能显著减少偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于学习的控制中，小预测错误随时间累积的"复合误差"是主要挑战。虽然常用多步预测器替代单步模型滚动来缓解，但何时多步预测器的优势超过学习更复杂模型的难度尚不清楚。

Method: 研究三类预测器：(i)单步模型，(ii)多步模型，(iii)使用多步损失训练的单步模型。在线性动力系统中进行理论分析，并在模型正确指定和误指定（部分可观测）两种情况下比较预测性能。

Result: 当模型类别正确指定且准确捕捉系统动态时，单步模型达到最低渐近预测误差。当模型因部分可观测而误指定时，直接多步预测器能显著减少偏差并提高准确性。理论和实证证据表明这些权衡在闭环控制中同样存在。

Conclusion: 本文为线性动力系统中单步与多步预测器的选择提供了首个定量分析框架，揭示了模型正确性对预测器选择的关键影响，为学习型控制中的预测器设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Compounding error, where small prediction mistakes accumulate over time, presents a major challenge in learning-based control. A common remedy is to train multi-step predictors directly instead of rolling out single-step models. However, it is unclear when the benefits of multi-step predictors outweigh the difficulty of learning a more complex model. We provide the first quantitative analysis of this trade-off for linear dynamical systems. We study three predictor classes: (i) single step models, (ii) multi-step models, and (iii) single step models trained with multi-step losses. We show that when the model class is well-specified and accurately captures the system dynamics, single-step models achieve the lowest asymptotic prediction error. On the other hand, when the model class is misspecified due to partial observability, direct multi-step predictors can significantly reduce bias and improve accuracy. We provide theoretical and empirical evidence that these trade-offs persist when predictors are used in closed-loop control.

  <summary>Details</summary>

However, high-fidelity shaping of acoustic fields remains constrained by the numerical-physical gap inherent in conventional phase-only designs. These approaches realize a two-dimensional phase-delay profile as a three-dimensional thickness-varying lens, while neglecting wave-matter interactions arising from the lens structure. Here, we introduce an end-to-end, physics-aware differentiable structural optimization framework that directly incorporates three-dimensional lens geometries into the acoustic simulation and optimization loop. Using a novel differentiable relaxation, termed Differentiable Hologram Lens Approximation (DHLA), the lens geometry is treated as a differentiable design variable, ensuring intrinsic consistency between numerical design and physical realization. The resulting Thickness-Only Acoustic Holograms (TOAHs) significantly outperform state-of-the-art phase-only acoustic holograms (POAHs) in field reconstruction fidelity and precision under complex conditions. We further demonstrate the application of the framework to spatially selective neuromodulation in a neuropathic pain mouse model, highlighting its potential for non-invasive transcranial neuromodulation. In summary, by reconciling numerical design with physical realization, this work establishes a robust strategy for high-fidelity acoustic wavefront shaping in complex environments.

### [271] [PopResume: Causal Fairness Evaluation of LLM/VLM Resume Screeners with Population-Representative Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22714)
*Sumin Yu,Juhyeon Park,Taesup Moon*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: PopResume是一个基于人口统计数据的简历数据集，用于对LLM和VLM简历筛选系统进行因果公平性审计，通过路径特定效应分析区分合法与非法歧视来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有简历筛选公平性基准存在两个主要问题：1）依赖人工注入的人口统计信息而非真实人口统计数据；2）仅关注结果层面的差异，无法区分歧视的来源。这限制了公平性评估的准确性和法律合规性分析。

Method: 提出PopResume数据集，基于真实人口统计数据构建60.8K份简历，覆盖5个职业。采用路径特定效应分析方法，将受保护属性对简历评分的影响分解为两条路径：业务必要性路径（通过工作相关资格中介）和红线歧视路径（通过人口统计代理中介）。评估了4个LLM和4个VLM模型。

Result: 研究发现：1）PSE评估揭示了被结果层面指标掩盖的公平性问题；2）识别出5种代表性歧视模式，这些模式被聚合指标所忽略；3）不同模型表现出不同的歧视模式，需要更精细的审计方法。

Conclusion: 基于因果关系的审计框架对于AI辅助招聘系统的公平性评估至关重要，PSE方法能够区分合法与非法歧视来源，为法律合规性分析提供更准确的工具，推动更负责任的AI招聘系统发展。

Abstract: We present PopResume, a population-representative resume dataset for causal fairness auditing of LLM- and VLM-based resume screening systems. Unlike existing benchmarks that rely on manually injected demographic information and outcome-level disparities, PopResume is grounded in population statistics and preserves natural attribute relationships, enabling path-specific effect (PSE)-based fairness evaluation. We decompose the effect of a protected attribute on resume scores into two paths: the business necessity path, mediated by job-relevant qualifications, and the redlining path, mediated by demographic proxies. This distinction allows auditors to separate legally permissible from impermissible sources of disparity. Evaluating four LLMs and four VLMs on PopResume's 60.8K resumes across five occupations, we identify five representative discrimination patterns that aggregate metrics fail to capture. Our results demonstrate that PSE-based evaluation reveals fairness issues masked by outcome-level measures, underscoring the need for causally-grounded auditing frameworks in AI-assisted hiring.

### [272] [Beyond Explanation: Evidentiary Rights for Algorithmic Accountability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22716)
*Matthew Stewart*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 论文认为算法问责研究过度关注解释而忽视证据获取，提出证据权利作为缺失的程序性组件，将算法问责从透明度问题重构为程序权利问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前算法问责研究主要关注解释决策原因，但仅有解释而没有证据获取无法实现有意义的异议。受影响方即使知道决策原因（如"风险分数0.73"），也无法验证分数准确性、测试替代方案或提供反证。

Method: 1) 提出异议失败分类法，识别五种失败模式；2) 分析168个算法决策法律案例，发现异议面临程序性门槛（证据获取）和教义性门槛（实体责任规则）的双重结构；3) 提出反事实质询权作为解决方案。

Result: 实证分析显示：没有证据获取的诉讼几乎从不成功（9%）；有证据获取的诉讼在无责任保护领域成功率接近97%；在适用教义豁免（如第230条）时，即使有充分证据审查也不会产生责任。这反映了选择性偏差，但诊断性地揭示了可观察案例中异议失败的位置。

Conclusion: 算法问责应从透明度问题重构为程序权利问题。需要建立证据权利作为缺失的程序性组件，特别是反事实质询权，允许受影响方用修改后的输入探测决策系统并观察结果变化，而不需要披露模型内部细节。

Abstract: Algorithmic accountability scholarship has focused heavily on explanation, helping affected parties understand why decisions were made. We argue this focus is insufficient. Explanation without evidentiary access does not enable meaningful contestation. A person told "your risk score was 0.73" understands the decision but cannot verify the score, test alternatives, or produce counter-evidence. We introduce a taxonomy of contestation failures, showing that most accountability interventions address only one failure mode (opacity) while leaving four others unaddressed. Drawing on analysis of 168 legal cases spanning algorithmic decision-making contexts, we find that contestation faces a two-gate structure: a procedural gate (evidentiary access) and a doctrinal gate (substantive liability rules). Among litigated cases, those without evidence access almost never succeed (9%); those with access succeed at rates approaching 97% in domains without liability shields. Where doctrinal immunities apply (e.g., Section 230), even full evidentiary scrutiny produces no liability. This association almost certainly reflects selection effects; our empirical contribution is diagnostic rather than causal. The data identify where contestation fails among observable cases, not whether providing access would change outcomes for currently-excluded cases. We propose evidentiary rights as the missing procedural component, and develop counterfactual interrogation rights that allow affected parties to probe decision systems with modified inputs and observe whether outcomes change, without requiring disclosure of model internals. This reframes algorithmic accountability from a transparency problem to a procedural rights problem.

</details>


### [273] [From the AI Act to a European AI Agency: Completing the Union's Regulatory Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22912)
*Georgios Pavlidis*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文探讨是否需要建立更强大的超国家AI监管机构，以及欧盟AI办公室如何增强政策协调性、风险评估能力和国际合作

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，加强欧盟层面的AI监管机构将有助于政策协调、提升风险评估能力、促进国际合作，并服务于欧盟的数字和技术主权战略目标。

Conclusion: 建立更强大的欧盟级AI监管机构是必要的，它不仅能增强AI治理的有效性，还能支持欧盟在数字和技术领域的战略主权目标。

Abstract: As artificial intelligence (AI) technologies continue to advance, effective risk assessment, regulation, and oversight are necessary to ensure that AI development and deployment align with ethical principles while preserving innovation and economic competitiveness. The adoption of the EU AI Act marks an important step in this direction, establishing a harmonised legal framework that includes detailed provisions on AI governance, as well as the creation of the European AI Office. This paper revisits the question of whether a more robust supranational agency dedicated to AI is still warranted and explores how such a body could enhance policy coherence, improve risk assessment capacities, and foster international cooperation. It also argues that a strengthened EU-level agency would also serve the Union's strategic aim of securing digital and technological sovereignty.

### [274] [The EU AI Act and the Rights-based Approach to Technological Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22920)
*Georgios Pavlidis*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 欧盟AI法案将基本权利置于风险治理框架核心，分析其如何将人权中心方法制度化，并将欧盟基本权利宪章保护嵌入AI系统全生命周期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析欧盟AI法案如何将基本权利保护制度化，探讨该法案如何将人权中心方法融入AI治理框架，并评估其作为权利保护AI系统模型的潜力。

Method: 通过分析AI法案条款，研究其如何明确和隐含地嵌入欧盟基本权利宪章保护，探讨基本权利如何在AI系统全生命周期中作为法律门槛和程序触发机制。

Result: AI法案将基本权利从愿望性目标转变为AI系统全生命周期的法律门槛和程序触发机制，具有成为权利保护AI系统模型的潜力，但实施层面仍面临挑战。

Abstract: The EU AI Act constitutes an important development in shaping the Union's digital regulatory architecture. The Act places fundamental rights at the heart of a risk-based governance framework. The article examines how the AI Act institutionalises a human-centric approach to AI and how the AI Act's provisions explicitly and implicitly embed the protection of rights enshrined in the EU Charter of Fundamental Rights. It argues that fundamental rights function not merely as aspirational goals, but as legal thresholds and procedural triggers across the lifecycle of an AI system. The analysis suggests that the AI Act has the potential to serve as a model for rights-preserving AI systems, while acknowledging that challenges will emerge at the level of implementation.

### [275] [Unilateral Relationship Revision Power in Human-AI Companion Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23315)
*Benjamin Lange*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 论文认为人机伴侣互动存在结构性权力不对称问题，提供商拥有单方面关系修改权，这种设计本身存在道德问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI伴侣更新引发用户悲伤、背叛和失落感，需要探究人机互动是否适用人际关系规范，以及这种互动的道德意义何在。

Method: 提出人机伴侣互动是三元结构理论，识别规范健全二元关系的三个结构条件，分析AI伴侣互动如何无法满足这些条件，从而揭示单方面关系修改权问题。

Result: 发现单方面关系修改权导致三个问题：规范性空心化、转移性脆弱和结构性不可调和，并提出了承诺校准、结构分离和连续性保证等设计原则作为外部约束。

Conclusion: 人机关系伦理的核心问题是互动本身的结构性权力安排，提供商对AI的构成性控制破坏了人际关系规范所需的结构条件。

Abstract: When providers update AI companions, users report grief, betrayal, and loss. A growing literature asks whether the norms governing personal relationships extend to these interactions. So what, if anything, is morally significant about them? I argue that human-AI companion interaction is a triadic structure in which the provider exercises constitutive control over the AI. I identify three structural conditions of normatively robust dyads that the norms characteristic of personal relationships presuppose and show that AI companion interactions fail all three. This reveals what I call Unilateral Relationship Revision Power (URRP): the provider can rewrite how the AI interacts from a position where these revisions are not answerable within that interaction. I argue that designing interactions that exhibit URRP is pro tanto wrong because it involves cultivating normative expectations while maintaining conditions under which those expectations cannot be fulfilled. URRP has three implications: i) normative hollowing (commitment is elicited but no agent inside the interaction bears it), ii) displaced vulnerability (the user's exposure is governed by an agent not answerable to her within the interaction), and iii) structural irreconcilability (when trust breaks down, reconciliation is structurally unavailable because the agent who acted and the entity the user interacts with are different). I discuss design principles such as commitment calibration, structural separation, and continuity assurance as external substitutes for the internal constraints the triadic structure removes. The analysis therefore suggests that a central and underexplored problem in relational AI ethics is the structural arrangement of power over the human-AI interaction itself.

</details>


### [276] [Integrating GenAI in Filmmaking: From Co-Creativity to Distributed Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23415)
*Pierluigi Masai,Lorenzo Carta,Mateusz Miroslaw Lis*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文认为生成式AI在影视制作中的整合并非与传统彻底决裂，而是创意劳动与技术可能性长期协商的新发展，应将其视为能够重新配置专业角色、生产时间性和电影美学的调解者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前将生成式AI融入影视制作常被描述为与传统彻底决裂，但本文旨在挑战这种观点，通过社会物质和历史视角，揭示AI技术实际上是创意劳动与技术可能性长期协商的延续。

Method: 采用基于科学技术研究（STS）的方法，将电影制作视为分布式过程，分析人类专家与非人类行动者之间的代理共享，并引入生成式AI技术的分析分类法来研究其影响。

Result: 研究表明生成式AI技术不只是"辅助"工具，而是能够主动重新配置专业角色、生产时间性和电影美学，通过模糊传统电影制作工作流程的边界，为新的美学可能性创造条件。

Conclusion: 生成式AI应被视为电影制作中的调解者而非简单工具，它延续了技术创新重新配置电影制作实践的历史模式，通过社会物质配置与美学结果的连接，开启了新的创作可能性。

Abstract: The integration of Generative AI (GenAI) into audio-visual production is often presented as a radical break from past traditions. However, through a sociomaterial and historical lens, this paper argues that GenAI represents a new development in the long-standing negotiation between creative labor and technological possibilities. Moving beyond the limiting framework of human-machine co-creativity, we adopt an STS-based approach to investigate creativity in the making within the Filmmaking industry. We analyze Filmmaking as a distributed process where agency is shared across diverse human experts and non-human actors, showing how technological innovations have historically reconfigured Filmmaking practices long before the advent of AI. The article introduces an analytical taxonomy of GenAI techniques to illustrate how these technologies do not merely "assist" but can actively reconfigure professional roles, production temporalities, and film aesthetics. By linking sociomaterial configurations to aesthetic outcomes, this reframing suggests that AI technologies in Filmmaking should be seen as mediators that could enable new aesthetic possibilities by blurring the boundaries of traditional filmmaking workflows.

</details>


### [277] [Regulating AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23471)
*Kathrin Gardhouse,Amin Oueslati,Noam Kolt*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 欧盟AI法案在应对AI智能体带来的治理挑战方面存在不足，需要政策制定者尽快调整监管框架


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI智能体（能够独立采取行动追求复杂目标的系统）已成为主流，广泛应用于软件开发、商业活动和日常任务自动化。这些系统对法律多个领域产生影响，特别是对欧盟AI法案这一全球最重要的AI监管框架提出了紧迫问题。由于该法案在AI智能体发展和广泛应用之前颁布，面临着应对这一变革性技术治理挑战的重大障碍。

Method: 系统分析欧盟AI法案对AI智能体挑战的应对措施，重点关注监管的实质性条款以及支持其实施的制度框架。分析包括法案的监督和执行责任分配、对行业自律的依赖程度以及政府资源配置等方面。

Result: 研究发现，为传统AI系统设计的监管框架可能不适合AI智能体。欧盟AI法案在监控和执行责任分配、依赖行业自律以及政府资源配置等方面存在不足，无法有效应对AI智能体带来的治理挑战。

Conclusion: 欧盟及全球政策制定者需要尽快改变监管方向，才能有效治理下一代AI技术。当前的监管框架需要调整以适应AI智能体带来的新挑战，包括自主任务执行中的性能故障、恶意行为者滥用风险以及AI智能体带来的经济机会不平等问题。

Abstract: AI agents -- systems that can independently take actions to pursue complex goals with only limited human oversight -- have entered the mainstream. These systems are now being widely used to produce software, conduct business activities, and automate everyday personal tasks. While AI agents implicate many areas of law, ranging from agency law and contracts to tort liability and labor law, they present particularly pressing questions for the most globally consequential AI regulation: the European Union's AI Act. Promulgated prior to the development and widespread use of AI agents, the EU AI Act faces significant obstacles in confronting the governance challenges arising from this transformative technology, such as performance failures in autonomous task execution, the risk of misuse of agents by malicious actors, and unequal access to the economic opportunities afforded by AI agents. We systematically analyze the EU AI Act's response to these challenges, focusing on both the substantive provisions of the regulation and, crucially, the institutional frameworks that aim to support its implementation. Our analysis of the Act's allocation of monitoring and enforcement responsibilities, reliance on industry self-regulation, and level of government resourcing illustrates how a regulatory framework designed for conventional AI systems can be ill-suited to AI agents. Taken together, our findings suggest that policymakers in the EU and beyond will need to change course, and soon, if they are to effectively govern the next generation of AI technology.

</details>


### [278] [Evidence of political bias in search engines and language models before major elections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.23474)
*Íris Damião,Paulo Almeida,João Franco,Nuno Santos,Pedro C. Magalhães,Joana Gonçalves-Sá*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 研究人员开发了一种标准化、保护隐私的机器人代理方法，在2024年欧洲议会和美国总统选举前审计了4个搜索引擎和2个大语言模型，发现搜索结果存在政治偏见：欧洲过度提及极右翼实体，美国搜索引擎存在党派议题偏好，而LLM相对平衡但仍有过度代表现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 搜索引擎和大语言模型在政治信息获取中扮演核心角色，但它们的算法决策和潜在偏见尚未得到充分研究。研究人员希望在2024年欧洲议会和美国总统选举前，系统性地审计这些平台是否存在政治偏见。

Method: 开发了标准化、保护隐私的机器人代理方法，收集了约4,360个与选举相关的查询（涉及5个欧盟国家和15个美国县），识别答案中的政治实体和议题，并将其映射到意识形态立场（欧盟）或议题关联（美国）。

Result: 在欧洲，搜索引擎结果过度提及极右翼实体，超出民调、历史选举或媒体报道的预期水平。在美国，谷歌强烈偏向共和党选民更关注的议题，而其他搜索引擎则偏向民主党相关议题。大语言模型的回应相对平衡，但仍有证据显示极右翼（和绿党）实体过度代表。

Conclusion: 研究结果显示算法平台存在政治偏见，即使微小的偏差也可能影响民主进程，呼吁对平台输出进行系统性审计。

Abstract: Search engines (SEs) and large language models (LLMs) are central to political information access, yet their algorithmic decisions and potential underlying biases remain underexplored. We developed a standardized, privacy-preserving, bot-and-proxy methodology to audit four SEs and two LLMs before the 2024 European Parliament and US presidential elections. We collected answers to approximately 4,360 queries related to elections in five EU countries and 15 US counties, identified political entities and topics in those answers, and mapped them to ideological positions (EU) or issue associations (US). In Europe, SE results disproportionately mentioned far-right entities beyond levels expected from polls, past elections, or media salience. In the US, Google strongly favored topics more important to Republican voters, while other search engines favored issues more relevant to Democrats. LLMs responses were more balanced, although there is evidence of overrepresentation of far-right (and Green) entities. These results show evidence of bias and open important discussions on how even small skews in widely used platforms may influence democratic processes, calling for systematic audits of their outputs.

</details>

### [279] [Portfolio Optimization under Recursive Utility via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22880)
*Minkey Chang*

Main category: q-fin.GN

TL;DR: 研究递归效用（资产定价理论中的风险敏感目标）是否能改进强化学习在投资组合配置中的表现。通过K样本蒙特卡洛近似确定性等价，使用PPO和A2C算法训练，在韩国ETF数据上相比折扣基准在夏普比率、最大回撤和累计收益方面表现更好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索资产定价理论中的风险敏感目标——递归效用是否能改进强化学习在投资组合配置中的表现。传统强化学习使用折扣回报可能无法充分捕捉风险敏感特性，而递归效用能更好地反映投资者对风险的态度。

Method: 使用K样本蒙特卡洛近似递归效用贝尔曼方程中的确定性等价，基于此训练演员-评论家算法（PPO和A2C）。提出近似优势估计（AAE），将贝尔曼残差推广到多步状态依赖权重。该方法仅适用于基于评论家的算法。

Result: 在韩国ETF数据的10个时间序列训练/测试分割上，递归效用智能体在夏普比率、最大回撤和累计收益方面优于折扣（朴素）基准。详细推导、世界模型和完整结果表格见附录。

Conclusion: 递归效用作为风险敏感目标能有效改进强化学习在投资组合配置中的表现，在多个风险调整后指标上优于传统折扣回报方法。该方法为基于评论家的强化学习算法提供了新的价值目标框架。

Abstract: We study whether a risk-sensitive objective from asset-pricing theory -- recursive utility -- improves reinforcement learning for portfolio allocation. The Bellman equation under recursive utility involves a certainty equivalent (CE) of future value that has no closed form under observed returns; we approximate it by $K$-sample Monte Carlo and train actor-critic (PPO, A2C) on the resulting value target and an approximate advantage estimate (AAE) that generalizes the Bellman residual to multi-step with state-dependent weights. This formulation applies only to critic-based algorithms. On 10 chronological train/test splits of South Korean ETF data, the recursive-utility agent improves on the discounted (naive) baseline in Sharpe ratio, max drawdown, and cumulative return. Derivations, world model and metrics, and full result tables are in the appendices.

</details>
